msg:Overall, it exceeded my expectations. During the May Day holiday, the prices of first-line lake view hotels increased a lot, so I blindly chose this family hotel. I didn't have much expectation, but I was very surprised after checking in:
Advantages: The hotel is in a good location, about 2km away from Hanling Old Street, and those with good physical strength can walk. It is also close to the International Lake House and the water camp. There is a bicycle rental shop at the door of the hotel, which is very convenient for those who don't want to drive. The hotel has a beautiful environment inside, and there is a lake at the door. Our room is on the first floor and has a small courtyard. The waiters will take the initiative to greet the guests when they see them. We stayed for two nights, and the housekeeper called every day to ask about the stay experience and needs. I said that the room temperature was too low and the air conditioner could not be adjusted. They immediately arranged to send an oil heater for heating. Thumbs up! The soy milk and various porridges for breakfast are quite special. Every morning, there are staff members who dress up as cartoon characters and send balloons at the entrance of the restaurant. Children love it the most. Of course, there are some shortcomings: the big slide in the children's playground costs 99 yuan to enter, which is a bit high... The room does not actively provide shower caps, face masks, etc., only toothbrushes and combs, and the paper used is too thin. Such thin paper needs to be used several times at a time, which does not really reduce the cost. üòÇ In addition, there are few restaurants around. It was too congested to drive out during the May Day holiday, so I could only solve it in the hotel's Chinese restaurant. The dishes are still good, but the price is a bit high. The hot spring is not well prepared, and I didn't experience it. It should be good. Overall, it is still a good hotel and I will consider staying again.
